        (se): Identity()
      )
      (2): Bottleneck(
        (conv1): Conv2d(2048, 512, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1), bias=False)

        (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)
        (se): Identity()
      )
    )
  )
  (heads): EmbeddingHead(
    (pool_layer): GlobalAvgPool(output_size=1)

    )
    (cls_layer): Linear(num_classes=36935, scale=1, margin=0.0)
  )
)
